aerial surveillance continued until the agreement was completely carried out.</span></p></td><td class="cl-94c975fa"><p class="cl-94c93bee"><span class="cl-94c930f4">United</span><span resolution.</span></p></td><td class="cl-94c975fc"><p class="cl-94c93bee"><span class="cl-94c930e0">No</span><span class="cl-94c930e0"> </span><span class="cl-94c930e0">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr in easing tensions between crisis actors which contributed to a more rapid termination of the crisis.</span></p></td><td class="cl-94c975fa"><p class="cl-94c93bee"><span Kennedy sent Dean Acheson to Paris on 23 October to brief NATO's Permanent Council on U.S. measures against Cuba.</span></p></td><td class="cl-94c975fc"><p class="cl-94c93bee"><span class="cl-94c930e0">No</span><span class="cl-94c930e0"> </span><span class="cl-94c930e0">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-94c9760f"><p class="cl-94c93bee"><span class="cl-94c930e0">196.38</span></p></td><td class="cl-94c9760e"><p class="cl-94c93bee"><span class="cl-94c930e0">Involved were members of the Warsaw Pact, whose forces were put on alert, and Latin American states which offered military assistance to the U.S.</span></p></td><td class="cl-94c9760e"><p class="cl-94c93bee"><span class="cl-94c930e0">No</span><span class="cl-94c930e0"> </span><span class="cl-94c930e0">events.</span></p></td></tr></tbody></table></div>

</span><span class="cl-94ef98e8">this</span><span class="cl-94ef98e8"> </span><span class="cl-94ef98e8">sentence</span><span class="cl-94ef98de">.</span><span class="cl-94ef98de"> </span><span interests of both the Greek and Turkish communities in Cyprus were recognized and safeguarded under a republican form of government, with several provisions insuring the fair participation of both autonomous communities in legislative functions.</span></p></td><td class="cl-95026734"><p class="cl-9502244a"><span class="cl-950217e8">No</span><span class="cl-950217e8"> </span><span class="cl-950217e8">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-95026740"><p class="cl-9502244a"><span class="cl-950217e8">202.4</span></p></td><td class="cl-9502673f"><p class="cl-9502244a"><span class="cl-950217e8">Once Cyprus became independent, however, each community became suspicious of the other's intentions.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9502673f"><p class="cl-9502244a"><span class="cl-950217e8">No</span><span class="cl-950217e8"> </span><span class="cl-950217e8">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr  --  through Johnsons pleas to all actors and warning to Turkey that it would no longer automatically be under U.S. protection if it should invade Cyprus  --  was the most effective southern part became the Kingdom of Burundi, and the northern part became the Republic of Rwanda.</span></p></td><td class="cl-95238978"><p class="cl-95235f3e"><span class="cl-95235340">No</span><span failed.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9523896e"><p class="cl-95235f3e"><span class="cl-95235340">No</span><span class="cl-95235340"> </span><span class="cl-95235340">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr
